class="docMainContainer_a9sJ"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_Qr34"><div class="docItemContainer_tjFy"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_T5ub" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a aria-label="Home page" class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="breadcrumbHomeIcon_sfvy"><path d="M10 19v-5h4v5c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1v-7h1.7c.46 0 .68-.57.33-.87L12.67 3.6c-.38-.34-.96-.34-1.34 0l-8.36 7.53c-.34.3-.13.87.33.87H5v7c0 .55.45 1 1 1h3c.55 0 1-.45 1-1z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/"><span>Assertions &amp; metrics</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Deterministic Metrics for LLM Output Validation</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_wXna theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_Ojys"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_iI2p">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><div style="position:relative"><header><h1>Deterministic metrics</h1></header>
<p>These metrics are created by logical tests that are run on LLM output.</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Assertion Type</th><th>Returns true if...</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><a href="#assert-set" class="">assert-set</a></td><td>A configurable threshold of grouped assertions pass</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#classifier" class="">classifier</a></td><td>HuggingFace classifier returns expected class above threshold</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains" class="">contains</a></td><td>output contains substring</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-all" class="">contains-all</a></td><td>output contains all list of substrings</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-any" class="">contains-any</a></td><td>output contains any of the listed substrings</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-json" class="">contains-json</a></td><td>output contains valid json (optional json schema validation)</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-html" class="">contains-html</a></td><td>output contains HTML content</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-sql" substrings, case insensitive</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#contains-any" class="">icontains-any</a></td><td>output contains any of the listed substrings, case insensitive</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#is-html" class="">is-html</a></td><td>output is valid HTML</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#is-json" class="">is-json</a></td><td>output is valid json (optional json schema vs expected tool calls</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#is-xml" class="">is-xml</a></td><td>output is valid xml</td></tr><tr><td><a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/javascript/">javascript</a></td><td>provided Javascript function validates the output</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#latency" threshold</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#perplexity-score" class="">perplexity-score</a></td><td>Normalized perplexity</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#perplexity" class="">perplexity</a></td><td>Perplexity is below a threshold</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#pi" class="">pi</a></td><td>Pi Labs scorer returns score above threshold</td></tr><tr><td><a class="" {pass: true}</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_WCGJ alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>tip</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Every test type can be negated by prepending <code>not-</code>. For example, <code>not-equals</code> or <code>not-regex</code>.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="assertion-types">Assertion types<a href="#assertion-types" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Assertion types" title="Direct link to Assertion types" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains">Contains<a href="#contains" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains" title="Direct link to Contains" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains</code> assertion checks if the LLM output contains the expected value.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;The expected substring&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The <code>icontains</code> is the same, except it ignores case:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> icontains</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;The expected substring&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-all">Contains-All<a href="#contains-all" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-All" title="Direct link to Contains-All" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains-all</code> assertion checks if the LLM output contains all of the specified values.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">all</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 2&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 3&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-any">Contains-Any<a href="#contains-any" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-Any" title="Direct link to Contains-Any" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains-any</code> assertion checks if the LLM output contains at least one of the specified values.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">any</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 2&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Value 3&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>For case insensitive matching, use <code>icontains-any</code>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="regex">Regex<a href="#regex" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Regex" title="Direct link to Regex" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>regex</code> assertion checks if the LLM output matches the provided regular expression.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> regex</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;\\d{4}&quot;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Matches a 4-digit number</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-json">Contains-JSON<a href="#contains-json" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-JSON" title="Direct link to Contains-JSON" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains-json</code> assertion checks if the LLM output contains a valid JSON structure.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">json</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You may optionally set a <code>value</code> as a JSON schema in order to validate the JSON contents:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">json</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">required</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> latitude</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> longitude</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> object</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">properties</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">latitude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">minimum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-90</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> number</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maximum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">90</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">longitude</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">minimum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-180</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> number</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maximum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">180</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>JSON is valid YAML, so you can also just copy in any JSON schema directly:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;required&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;latitude&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;longitude&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;type&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;object&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;properties&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;latitude&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;type&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;number&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;minimum&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-90</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;maximum&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">90</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;longitude&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;type&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;number&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;minimum&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-180</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;maximum&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">180</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>If your JSON schema is large, import it from a file:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">json</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//./path/to/schema.json</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>See also: <a href="#is-json" class=""><code>is-json</code></a></p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-html">Contains-Html<a href="#contains-html" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-Html" title="Direct link to Contains-Html" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains-html</code> assertion checks if the LLM output contains HTML content. This is useful when you want to verify that the model has generated HTML markup, even if it&#x27;s embedded within other text.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">html</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The assertion uses multiple indicators to detect HTML:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Opening and closing tags (e.g., <code>&lt;div&gt;</code>, <code>&lt;/div&gt;</code>)</li>
<li class="">Self-closing tags (e.g., <code>&lt;br /&gt;</code>, <code>&lt;img /&gt;</code>)</li>
<li class="">HTML entities (e.g., <code>&amp;amp;</code>, <code>&amp;nbsp;</code>, <code>&amp;#123;</code>)</li>
<li class="">HTML attributes (e.g., <code>class=&quot;example&quot;</code>, <code>id=&quot;test&quot;</code>)</li>
<li class="">HTML comments (e.g., <code>&lt;!-- comment --&gt;</code>)</li>
<li class="">DOCTYPE declarations</li>
</ul>
<p>This assertion requires at least two HTML indicators to avoid false positives from text like &quot;a &lt; b&quot; or email addresses.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-html">Is-Html<a href="#is-html" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Is-Html" title="Direct link to Is-Html" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>is-html</code> assertion checks if the entire LLM output is valid HTML (not just contains HTML fragments). The output must start and end with HTML tags, with no non-HTML content outside the tags.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">html</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This assertion will pass for:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Complete HTML documents: <code>&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;&lt;html&gt;...&lt;/html&gt;</code></li>
<li class="">HTML fragments: <code>&lt;div&gt;Content&lt;/div&gt;</code></li>
<li class="">Multiple elements: <code>&lt;h1&gt;Title&lt;/h1&gt;&lt;p&gt;Paragraph&lt;/p&gt;</code></li>
<li class="">Self-closing tags: <code>&lt;img src=&quot;test.jpg&quot; /&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<p>It will fail for:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Plain text: <code>Just text</code></li>
<li class="">Mixed content: <code>Text before &lt;div&gt;HTML&lt;/div&gt; text after</code></li>
<li class="">XML documents: <code>&lt;?xml version=&quot;1.0&quot;?&gt;&lt;root&gt;...&lt;/root&gt;</code></li>
<li class="">Incomplete HTML: <code>&lt;div&gt;Unclosed div</code></li>
<li class="">Non-HTML content with HTML inside: <code>Here is some HTML: &lt;div&gt;test&lt;/div&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-sql">Contains-Sql<a href="#contains-sql" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-Sql" title="Direct link to Contains-Sql" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>This assertion ensure that the output is either valid SQL, or contains a code block with valid SQL.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sql</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>See <a href="#is-sql" class=""><code>is-sql</code></a> for advanced usage, including specific database types and allowlists for tables and columns.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="cost">Cost<a href="#cost" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Cost" title="Direct link to Cost" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>cost</code> assertion checks if the cost of the LLM call is below a specified threshold.</p>
<p>This requires LLM providers to return cost information. Currently this is only supported by OpenAI GPT models and custom providers.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">mini</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Pass if the LLM call costs less than $0.001</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> cost</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.001</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="equality">Equality<a href="#equality" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Equality" title="Direct link to Equality" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>equals</code> assertion checks if the LLM output is equal to the expected value.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> equals</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;The expected output&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can also check whether it matches the expected JSON format.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> equals</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;key&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;value&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>If your expected JSON is large, import it from a file:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> equals</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;file://path/to/expected.json&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-json">Is-JSON<a href="#is-json" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Is-JSON" title="Direct link to Is-JSON" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>is-json</code> assertion checks if the LLM output is a valid JSON string.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">json</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You may optionally set a <code>value</code> as a JSON schema. If set, the output will be validated against this schema:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">minimum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-90</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> number</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maximum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">90</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">-180</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> number</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maximum</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">180</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>JSON is valid YAML, so you can also just copy in any JSON schema directly:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <p>If your JSON schema is large, import it from a file:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">json</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> file</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//./path/to/schema.json</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-xml">Is-XML<a href="#is-xml" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Is-XML" title="Direct link to Is-XML" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>is-xml</code> assertion checks if the entire LLM output is a valid XML string. It can also verify the presence of specific elements within the XML structure.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This basic usage checks if the output is valid XML.</p>
<p>You can also specify required elements:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">requiredElements</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> root.child</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> root.sibling</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This checks if the XML is valid and contains the specified elements. The elements are specified as dot-separated paths, allowing for nested element checking.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="how-it-works">How it works<a href="#how-it-works" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to How it works" title="Direct link to How it works" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<ol>
<li class="">The assertion first attempts to parse the entire output as XML using a parser (fast-xml-parser).</li>
<li class="">If parsing succeeds, it&#x27;s considered valid XML.</li>
<li class="">If <code>value</code> is specified:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="">It checks for a requiredElements key with an array of required elements.</li>
<li class="">Each element path (e.g., &quot;root.child&quot;) is split by dots.</li>
<li class="">It traverses the parsed XML object following these paths.</li>
<li class="">If any required element is not found, the assertion fails.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="examples">Examples<a href="#examples" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Examples" title="Direct link to Examples" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Basic XML validation:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Passes for: <code>&lt;root&gt;&lt;child&gt;Content&lt;/child&gt;&lt;/root&gt;</code>
Fails for: <code>&lt;root&gt;&lt;child&gt;Content&lt;/child&gt;&lt;/root</code> (missing closing tag)</p>
<p>Checking for specific elements:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">requiredElements</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> analysis.classification</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> analysis.color</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Passes for: <code>&lt;analysis&gt;&lt;classification&gt;T-shirt&lt;/classification&gt;&lt;color&gt;Red&lt;/color&gt;&lt;/analysis&gt;</code>
Fails for: <code>&lt;analysis&gt;&lt;classification&gt;T-shirt&lt;/classification&gt;&lt;/analysis&gt;</code> (missing color element)</p>
<p>Checking nested elements:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">requiredElements</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> root.parent.child.grandchild</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Passes for: <code>&lt;root&gt;&lt;parent&gt;&lt;child&gt;&lt;grandchild&gt;Content&lt;/grandchild&gt;&lt;/child&gt;&lt;/parent&gt;&lt;/root&gt;</code>
Fails for: <code>&lt;root&gt;&lt;parent&gt;&lt;child&gt;&lt;/child&gt;&lt;/parent&gt;&lt;/root&gt;</code> (missing grandchild element)</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="inverse-assertion">Inverse assertion<a href="#inverse-assertion" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Inverse assertion" title="Direct link to Inverse assertion" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>You can use the <code>not-is-xml</code> assertion to check if the output is not valid XML:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> not</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">xml</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This will pass for non-XML content and fail for valid XML content.</p>
<p>Note: The <code>is-xml</code> assertion requires the entire output to be valid XML. For checking XML content within a larger text, use the <code>contains-xml</code> assertion.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="contains-xml">Contains-XML<a href="#contains-xml" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Contains-XML" title="Direct link to Contains-XML" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>contains-xml</code> is identical to <code>is-xml</code>, except it checks if the LLM output contains valid XML content, even if it&#x27;s not the entire output. For example, the following is valid.</p>
<div class="language-xml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-xml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">Sure, here is your xml:</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token tag" style="color:#00009f">root</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token tag" style="color:#00009f">child</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token plain">Content</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&lt;/</span><span class="token tag" style="color:#00009f">child</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&lt;/</span><span class="token tag" style="color:#00009f">root</span><span class="token tag punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">let me know if you have any other questions!</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-sql">Is-SQL<a href="#is-sql" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Is-SQL" title="Direct link to Is-SQL" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>is-sql</code> assertion checks if the LLM output is a valid SQL statement.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sql</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>To use this assertion, you need to install the <code>node-sql-parser</code> package. You can install it using npm:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">npm</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">install</span><span class="token plain"> node-sql-parser</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can optionally set a <code>databaseType</code> in the <code>value</code> to determine the specific database syntax that your LLM output will be validated against. The default database syntax is MySQL. For a complete and up-to-date list of supported database syntaxes, please refer to the <a href="https://github.com/taozhi8833998/node-sql-parser?tab=readme-ov-file#supported-database-sql-syntax" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">node-sql-parser documentation</a>.<br>
<!-- -->The supported database syntax list:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Athena</li>
<li class="">BigQuery</li>
<li class="">DB2</li>
<li class="">FlinkSQL</li>
<li class="">Hive</li>
<li class="">MariaDB</li>
<li class="">MySQL</li>
<li class="">Noql</li>
<li class="">PostgresQL</li>
<li class="">Redshift</li>
<li class="">Snowflake(alpha)</li>
<li class="">Sqlite</li>
<li class="">TransactSQL</li>
</ul>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sql</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">databaseType</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;MySQL&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can also optionally set a <code>allowedTables</code>/<code>allowedColumns</code> in the <code>value</code> to determine the SQL authority list that your LLM output will be validated against.<br>
<!-- -->The format of allowedTables:</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{type}::{dbName}::{tableName} // type could be select, update, delete or insert</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The format of allowedColumns:</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">{type}::{tableName}::{columnName} // type could be select, update, delete or insert</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>For <code>SELECT *</code>, <code>DELETE</code>, and <code>INSERT INTO tableName VALUES()</code> without specified columns, the <code>.*</code> column authority regex is required.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">sql</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">databaseType</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;MySQL&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">allowedTables</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;(select|update|insert|delete)::null::departments&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">allowedColumns</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;select::null::name&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;update::null::id&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-valid-function-call">is-valid-function-call<a href="#is-valid-function-call" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to is-valid-function-call" title="Direct link to is-valid-function-call" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>This ensures that any JSON LLM output adheres to the schema specified in the <code>functions</code> configuration of the provider. This is implemented for a subset of providers. Learn more about the <a class="" href="/docs/providers/vertex/#function-calling-and-tools">Google Vertex provider</a>, <a class="" href="/docs/providers/google/#function-calling">Google AIStudio provider</a>, <a class="" href="/docs/providers/google/#function-calling-example">Google Live provider</a> and <a class="" href="/docs/providers/openai/#using-tools-and-functions">OpenAI provider</a>, which this is implemented for.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-valid-openai-function-call">is-valid-openai-function-call<a href="#is-valid-openai-function-call" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to is-valid-openai-function-call" title="Direct link to is-valid-openai-function-call" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Legacy - please use is-valid-function-call instead. This ensures that any JSON LLM output adheres to the schema specified in the <code>functions</code> configuration of the provider. Learn more about the <a class="" href="/docs/providers/openai/#using-tools-and-functions">OpenAI provider</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="is-valid-openai-tools-call">is-valid-openai-tools-call<a href="#is-valid-openai-tools-call" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to is-valid-openai-tools-call" title="Direct link to is-valid-openai-tools-call" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>This ensures that any JSON LLM output adheres to the schema specified in the <code>tools</code> configuration of the provider. Learn more about the <a class="" href="/docs/providers/openai/#using-tools-and-functions">OpenAI provider</a>.</p>
<p><strong>MCP Support</strong>: This assertion also validates MCP (Model Context Protocol) tool calls when using OpenAI&#x27;s Responses API. It will:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Pass if MCP tool calls succeed (output contains &quot;MCP Tool Result&quot;)</li>
<li class="">Fail if MCP tool calls fail (output contains &quot;MCP Tool Error&quot;)</li>
<li class="">Continue to validate traditional function tools as before</li>
</ul>
<p>Example with MCP tools:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span
