style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> mcp</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">server_label</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> deepwiki</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">server_url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//mcp.deepwiki.com/mcp</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">require_approval</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> never</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">query</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;What is MCP?&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> is</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">valid</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">call </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Validates MCP tool success</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> contains</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;MCP Tool Result&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Alternative way to check for MCP success</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="tool-call-f1">tool-call-f1<a href="#tool-call-f1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to tool-call-f1" title="Direct link to tool-call-f1" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>tool-call-f1</code> assertion computes the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F-score" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">F1 score</a> comparing the set of tools called by the LLM against an expected set of tools. This metric is useful for evaluating agentic LLM applications where you want to measure how accurately the model selects the right tools.</p>
<p>This assertion supports multiple provider formats including OpenAI, Anthropic, and Google/Vertex.</p>
<p>The F1 score is the harmonic mean of precision and recall, originally introduced by <a href="http://www.dcs.gla.ac.uk/Keith/Preface.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">van Rijsbergen (1979)</a> for information retrieval evaluation:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Precision</strong> = |actual ∩ expected| / |actual| — &quot;Of the tools called, how many were correct?&quot;</li>
<li class=""><strong>Recall</strong> = |actual ∩ expected| / |expected| — &quot;Of the expected tools, how many were called?&quot;</li>
<li class=""><strong>F1</strong> = 2 × (precision × recall) / (precision + recall)</li>
</ul>
<p>This uses <strong>unordered set comparison</strong> — only the presence of tool names matters, not the order or frequency of calls.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">4.1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tools</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> function</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> get_weather</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">parameters</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> object</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token key atrule" class="token plain">                </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">city</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">                  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> string</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> function</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">function</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> book_flight</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">            </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">parameters</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> object</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">              </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">properties</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">                </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">destination</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">                  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> string</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">query</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;What&#x27;s the weather in NYC and book me a flight to LA?&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Require exact match (F1 = 1.0)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> tool</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">call</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">f1</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> get_weather</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">          </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> book_flight</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Allow partial matches with custom threshold</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> tool</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">call</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">f1</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;get_weather&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;book_flight&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.8</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The <code>value</code> can be specified as:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">An array of tool names: <code>[&#x27;get_weather&#x27;, &#x27;book_flight&#x27;]</code></li>
<li class="">A comma-separated string: <code>&#x27;get_weather, book_flight&#x27;</code></li>
</ul>
<p>The <code>threshold</code> defaults to <code>1.0</code> (exact match required). Lower thresholds allow partial matches, which is useful during development or when some flexibility is acceptable.</p>
<p><strong>Scoring examples:</strong></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Expected Tools</th><th>Actual Tools Called</th><th>Precision</th><th>Recall</th><th>F1</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>[get_weather, book_flight]</code></td><td><code>[get_weather, book_flight]</code></td><td>1.0</td><td>1.0</td><td>1.0</td></tr><tr><td><code>[get_weather, book_flight]</code></td><td><code>[get_weather]</code></td><td>1.0</td><td>0.5</td><td>0.667</td></tr><tr><td><code>[get_weather, book_flight]</code></td><td><code>[get_weather, book_flight, search]</code></td><td>0.667</td><td>1.0</td><td>0.8</td></tr><tr><td><code>[get_weather]</code></td><td><code>[book_flight]</code></td><td>0.0</td><td>0.0</td><td>0.0</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="javascript">Javascript<a href="#javascript" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Javascript" title="Direct link to Javascript" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>See <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/javascript/">Javascript assertions</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="latency">Latency<a href="#latency" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Latency" title="Direct link to Latency" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>latency</code> assertion fails if the LLM call takes longer than the specified threshold. Duration is specified in milliseconds.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Fail if the LLM call takes longer than 5 seconds</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> latency</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5000</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Note that <code>latency</code> requires that the <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/caching/">cache is disabled</a> with <code>promptfoo eval --no-cache</code> or an equivalent option.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="levenshtein-distance">Levenshtein distance<a href="#levenshtein-distance" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Levenshtein distance" title="Direct link to Levenshtein distance" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>levenshtein</code> assertion checks if the LLM output is within a given edit distance from an expected value.</p>
<p>Levenshtein distance measures the number of single-character edits (insertions, deletions, or substitutions) required to change one string into another. This metric is useful for:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Fuzzy matching</strong>: When you want to allow minor typos or variations (e.g., &quot;color&quot; vs &quot;colour&quot;)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Name matching</strong>: When checking if the model outputs names correctly with some tolerance for spelling</li>
<li class=""><strong>Code generation</strong>: When verifying that generated code is close to expected output</li>
</ul>
<p>For example, the distance between &quot;kitten&quot; and &quot;sitting&quot; is 3 (substitute &#x27;k&#x27;→&#x27;s&#x27;, substitute &#x27;e&#x27;→&#x27;i&#x27;, insert &#x27;g&#x27;). <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Levenshtein_distance" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Learn more on Wikipedia</a>.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure Levenshtein distance from &quot;hello world&quot; is &lt;= 5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> levenshtein</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>value</code> can reference other variables using template syntax. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">expected</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> foobar</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> levenshtein</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{expected}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="perplexity">Perplexity<a href="#perplexity" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Perplexity" title="Direct link to Perplexity" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Perplexity measures how &quot;surprised&quot; a language model is by its own output. It&#x27;s calculated from the log probabilities of tokens, where lower values indicate higher model confidence.</p>
<p><strong>Key points:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Low perplexity</strong> = high confidence (model thinks its output is likely)</li>
<li class=""><strong>High perplexity</strong> = low confidence (often correlates with hallucination or confusion)</li>
<li class="">Useful for quality control and detecting when the model is uncertain</li>
</ul>
<p>The assertion passes when perplexity is <strong>below</strong> the threshold.</p>
<p>To specify a perplexity threshold, use the <code>perplexity</code> assertion type:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Fail if the LLM perplexity is above threshold (i.e., model is too confused)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> perplexity</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1.5</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Perplexity requires the LLM API to output <code>logprobs</code>. Currently only more recent versions of OpenAI GPT and Azure OpenAI GPT APIs support this.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="comparing-different-outputs-from-the-same-llm">Comparing different outputs from the same LLM<a href="#comparing-different-outputs-from-the-same-llm" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Comparing different outputs from the same LLM" title="Direct link to Comparing different outputs from the same LLM" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>You can compare perplexity scores across different outputs from the same model to get a sense of which output the model finds more likely (or less surprising). This is a good way to tune your prompts and hyperparameters (like temperature).</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="comparing-outputs-from-different-llms">Comparing outputs from different LLMs<a href="#comparing-outputs-from-different-llms" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Comparing outputs from different LLMs" title="Direct link to Comparing outputs from different LLMs" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Comparing scores across models may not be meaningful, unless the models have been trained on similar datasets, the tokenization process is consistent between models, and the vocabulary of the models is roughly the same.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="perplexity-score">perplexity-score<a href="#perplexity-score" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to perplexity-score" title="Direct link to perplexity-score" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p><code>perplexity-score</code> is a supported metric similar to <code>perplexity</code>, except it is normalized between 0 and 1 and inverted, meaning larger numbers are better.</p>
<p>This makes it easier to include in an aggregate promptfoo score, as higher scores are usually better. In this example, we compare perplexity across multiple GPTs:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">mini</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> openai</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">gpt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> perplexity</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">score</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.5</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># optional</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># ...</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="python">Python<a href="#python" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Python" title="Direct link to Python" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>See <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/python/">Python assertions</a>.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="starts-with">Starts-With<a href="#starts-with" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Starts-With" title="Direct link to Starts-With" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>starts-with</code> assertion checks if the LLM output begins with the specified string.</p>
<p>This example checks if the output starts with &quot;Yes&quot;:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> starts</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">with</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Yes&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="trace-span-count">Trace-Span-Count<a href="#trace-span-count" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Trace-Span-Count" title="Direct link to Trace-Span-Count" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>trace-span-count</code> assertion counts the number of spans in a trace that match a given pattern and checks if the count is within specified bounds. This is useful for validating that expected operations occurred in your LLM application.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Trace assertions require tracing to be enabled in your evaluation. See the <a class="" href="/docs/tracing/">tracing documentation</a> for setup instructions.</p><p>If trace data is not available, the assertion will throw an error rather than failing, indicating that the assertion could not be evaluated.</p></div></div>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure at least one LLM call was made</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">count</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation"
