style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*llm*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">min</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure no more than 5 database queries</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">count</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*database*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure exactly 2-4 retrieval operations</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">count</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*retrieve*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">min</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">4</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The <code>pattern</code> field supports glob-style matching:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>*</code> matches any sequence of characters</li>
<li class=""><code>?</code> matches any single character</li>
<li class="">Matching is case-insensitive</li>
</ul>
<p>Common patterns:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>*llm*</code> - Matches spans with &quot;llm&quot; anywhere in the name</li>
<li class=""><code>api.*</code> - Matches spans starting with &quot;api.&quot;</li>
<li class=""><code>*.error</code> - Matches spans ending with &quot;.error&quot;</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="trace-span-duration">Trace-Span-Duration<a href="#trace-span-duration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Trace-Span-Duration" title="Direct link to Trace-Span-Duration" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>trace-span-duration</code> assertion checks if span durations in a trace are within acceptable limits. It can check individual spans or percentiles across all matching spans.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>This assertion requires trace data to be available. If tracing is not enabled or trace data is missing, the assertion will throw an error.</p></div></div>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure all spans complete within 3 seconds</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">duration</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">3000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># milliseconds</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure LLM calls complete quickly (95th percentile)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">duration</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*llm*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2000</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">percentile</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">95</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Check 95th percentile instead of all spans</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure database queries are fast</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">span</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">duration</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*database.query*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">100</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Key features:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>pattern</code> (optional): Filter spans by name pattern. Defaults to <code>*</code> (all spans)</li>
<li class=""><code>max</code>: Maximum allowed duration in milliseconds</li>
<li class=""><code>percentile</code> (optional): Check percentile instead of all spans (e.g., 50 for median, 95 for 95th percentile)</li>
</ul>
<p>The assertion will show the slowest spans when a threshold is exceeded, making it easy to identify performance bottlenecks.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="trace-error-spans">Trace-Error-Spans<a href="#trace-error-spans" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Trace-Error-Spans" title="Direct link to Trace-Error-Spans" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>trace-error-spans</code> assertion detects error spans in a trace and ensures the error rate is within acceptable limits. It automatically detects errors through status codes, error attributes, and status messages.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>note</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>This assertion requires trace data to be available. If tracing is not enabled or trace data is missing, the assertion will throw an error.</p></div></div>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># No errors allowed</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">error</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">spans</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Backward compatible - simple number means max_count</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Allow at most 2 errors</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">error</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">spans</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_count</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Allow up to 5% error rate</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">error</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">spans</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_percentage</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">5</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Check errors only in API calls</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> trace</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">error</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">spans</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pattern</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;*api*&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_count</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Error detection methods:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Status codes</strong>: HTTP status codes &gt;= 400</li>
<li class=""><strong>Error attributes</strong>: Checks for <code>error</code>, <code>exception</code>, <code>failed</code>, <code>failure</code> attributes</li>
<li class=""><strong>OpenTelemetry standards</strong>: <code>otel.status_code: ERROR</code>, <code>status.code: ERROR</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>Status messages</strong>: Messages containing &quot;error&quot;, &quot;failed&quot;, &quot;exception&quot;, &quot;timeout&quot;, &quot;abort&quot;</li>
</ul>
<p>Configuration options:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>max_count</code>: Maximum number of error spans allowed</li>
<li class=""><code>max_percentage</code>: Maximum error rate as a percentage (0-100)</li>
<li class=""><code>pattern</code>: Filter spans by name pattern</li>
</ul>
<p>The assertion provides detailed error information including span names and error messages to help with debugging.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="webhook">Webhook<a href="#webhook" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Webhook" title="Direct link to Webhook" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>webhook</code> assertion sends the LLM output to a specified webhook URL for custom validation. The webhook should return a JSON object with a <code>pass</code> property set to <code>true</code> or <code>false</code>.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> webhook</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/webhook&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The webhook will receive a POST request with a JSON payload containing the LLM output and the context (test case variables). For example, if the LLM output is &quot;Hello, World!&quot; and the test case has a variable <code>example</code> set to &quot;Example text&quot;, the payload will look like:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;output&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Hello, World!&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;context&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;prompt&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Greet the user&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;vars&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;example&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Example text&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The webhook should process the request and return a JSON response with a <code>pass</code> property set to <code>true</code> or <code>false</code>, indicating whether the LLM output meets the custom validation criteria. Optionally, the webhook can also provide a <code>reason</code> property to describe why the output passed or failed the assertion.</p>
<p>Example response:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;pass&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;reason&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;The output meets the custom validation criteria&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>If the webhook returns a <code>pass</code> value of <code>true</code>, the assertion will be considered successful. If it returns <code>false</code>, the assertion will fail, and the provided <code>reason</code> will be used to describe the failure.</p>
<p>You may also return a score:</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;pass&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;score&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;reason&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;The output meets the custom validation criteria&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="rouge-n">Rouge-N<a href="#rouge-n" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Rouge-N" title="Direct link to Rouge-N" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>rouge-n</code> assertion checks if the Rouge-N score between the LLM output and expected value is above a given threshold.</p>
<p>ROUGE-N is a <strong>recall-oriented</strong> metric that measures how much of the reference text appears in the generated output. It counts overlapping n-grams (word sequences) between the two texts.</p>
<p><strong>What &quot;recall-oriented&quot; means:</strong> ROUGE-N asks &quot;How much of what should be there is actually there?&quot; - perfect for summarization tasks where you want to ensure key information isn&#x27;t missed.</p>
<p><strong>When to use ROUGE-N:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Summarization</strong>: Ensure summaries include key points from source text</li>
<li class=""><strong>Information extraction</strong>: Verify that important facts are captured</li>
<li class=""><strong>Content coverage</strong>: Check if the output mentions all required elements</li>
</ul>
<p>ROUGE stands for <strong>Recall-Oriented Understudy for Gisting Evaluation</strong>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ROUGE_(metric)" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Learn more on Wikipedia</a>.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure Rouge-N score compared to &quot;hello world&quot; is &gt;= 0.75 (default threshold)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> rouge</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">n</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># With custom threshold</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> rouge</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">n</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.6</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>value</code> can reference other variables using template syntax. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">expected</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> rouge</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">n</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{expected}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="bleu">BLEU<a href="#bleu" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to BLEU" title="Direct link to BLEU" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>BLEU (Bilingual Evaluation Understudy) is a <strong>precision-oriented</strong> metric originally designed for evaluating machine translation. Unlike ROUGE-N which asks &quot;is everything included?&quot;, BLEU asks &quot;is everything correct?&quot;</p>
<p><strong>What &quot;precision-oriented&quot; means:</strong> BLEU checks if the words in the generated output actually appear in the reference - it penalizes made-up or incorrect content.</p>
<p><strong>When to use BLEU:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Translation tasks</strong>: Ensure translations are accurate, not just complete</li>
<li class=""><strong>Factual generation</strong>: Verify the model isn&#x27;t hallucinating extra information</li>
<li class=""><strong>Concise outputs</strong>: When you want precise, accurate text without extra fluff</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>BLEU vs ROUGE-N:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>ROUGE-N</strong>: &quot;Did you mention everything important?&quot; (good for summaries)</li>
<li class=""><strong>BLEU</strong>: &quot;Is what you said actually correct?&quot; (good for translations)</li>
</ul>
<p>BLEU also includes a brevity penalty to discourage overly short outputs. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BLEU" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">See Wikipedia</a> for more background.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure BLEU score compared to &quot;hello world&quot; is &gt;= 0.5 (default threshold)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bleu</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># With custom threshold</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bleu</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>value</code> can reference other variables using template syntax. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">expected</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bleu</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{expected}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="gleu">GLEU<a href="#gleu" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to GLEU" title="Direct link to GLEU" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>GLEU (Google-BLEU) is designed specifically for evaluating <strong>individual sentences</strong>, fixing a major limitation of BLEU which was designed for large documents.</p>
<p><strong>Why GLEU instead of BLEU for sentences:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>No weird edge cases</strong>: BLEU can give misleading scores for short sentences due to its brevity penalty</li>
<li class=""><strong>Balanced evaluation</strong>: GLEU considers both precision AND recall, taking the minimum of both</li>
<li class=""><strong>Symmetrical</strong>: Swapping reference and output gives the same score (unlike BLEU)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Better for real-time evaluation</strong>: More reliable for evaluating single responses in chatbots or QA systems</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>How GLEU works differently:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">Records all n-grams (1-4 word sequences) from both texts</li>
<li class="">Calculates both precision (like BLEU) AND recall (like ROUGE)</li>
<li class="">Final score = minimum(precision, recall)</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>When to use GLEU:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Single response evaluation</strong>: Evaluating individual chatbot or model responses</li>
<li class=""><strong>Short text comparison</strong>: When comparing headlines, titles, or short answers</li>
<li class=""><strong>Balanced accuracy needs</strong>: When both precision and recall matter equally</li>
</ul>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Ensure GLEU score compared to &quot;hello world&quot; is &gt;= 0.5 (default threshold)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> gleu</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><code>value</code> can reference other variables using template syntax. For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span <p>You can also provide multiple reference strings for evaluation:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="meteor">METEOR<a href="#meteor" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to METEOR" title="Direct link to METEOR" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>METEOR (Metric for Evaluation of Translation with Explicit ORdering) is the most sophisticated text similarity metric, going beyond simple word matching to understand meaning.</p>
<p><strong>What makes METEOR special:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Understands synonyms</strong>: Recognizes that &quot;good&quot; and &quot;nice&quot; mean similar things</li>
<li class=""><strong>Handles word forms</strong>: Knows that &quot;running&quot; and &quot;ran&quot; are the same verb</li>
<li class=""><strong>Considers word order</strong>: Unlike other metrics, it penalizes scrambled sentences</li>
<li class=""><strong>Balanced scoring</strong>: Combines precision, recall, AND word order into a single score</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>When to use METEOR:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>High-quality translation</strong>: When semantic accuracy matters more than exact wording</li>
<li class=""><strong>Natural language understanding</strong>: Evaluating if the model truly &quot;gets&quot; the meaning</li>
<li class=""><strong>Flexible matching</strong>: When there are many valid ways to express the same idea</li>
</ul>
<p>For additional context, read about the metric on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/METEOR" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Wikipedia</a>.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Installation Required</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>METEOR requires the optional <code>natural</code> package. Install it before using METEOR assertions:</p><div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">npm</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">install</span><span class="token plain"> natural@^8.1.0</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><p>If the package is not installed, you&#x27;ll receive an error message with installation instructions when attempting to use METEOR assertions.</p></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="how-meteor-works">How METEOR Works<a href="#how-meteor-works" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to How METEOR Works" title="Direct link to How METEOR Works" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>METEOR evaluates text by:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">Matching unigrams (words) between the generated text and reference(s) using:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="">Exact matches (surface forms)</li>
<li class="">Word stems (e.g., &quot;running&quot; → &quot;run&quot;)</li>
<li class="">Semantic meanings</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="">Computing a final score (0.0 to 1.0) based on:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class="">Unigram precision (accuracy of matched words)</li>
<li class="">Unigram recall (coverage of reference words)</li>
<li class="">Word order/fragmentation (how well the word order matches)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-usage">Basic Usage<a href="#basic-usage" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Usage" title="Direct link to Basic Usage" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> meteor</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reference text to compare against</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>By default, METEOR uses a threshold of 0.5. Scores range from 0.0 (no match) to 1.0 (perfect match).</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="custom-threshold">Custom Threshold<a href="#custom-threshold" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Custom Threshold" title="Direct link to Custom Threshold" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Set your own threshold based on your quality requirements:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> meteor</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> hello world</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.7</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Test fails if score &lt; 0.7</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-variables">Using Variables<a href="#using-variables" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using Variables" title="Direct link to Using Variables" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Useful when your reference text comes from test data or external sources:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span meteor</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{reference_translation}}&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.6</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="multiple-references">Multiple References<a href="#multiple-references" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multiple References" title="Direct link to Multiple References" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>METEOR can evaluate against multiple reference texts, using the best-matching reference for scoring:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Hello world&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reference 1</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Hi there, world&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reference 2</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Greetings, world&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Reference 3</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">threshold</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.6</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This is particularly useful when:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Multiple valid translations/outputs exist</li>
<li class="">You&#x27;re working with different writing styles</li>
<li class="">You want to account for acceptable variations</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="practical-example">Practical Example<a href="#practical-example" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Practical Example" title="Direct link to Practical Example" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Here&#x27;s how METEOR scores different outputs against the reference &quot;The weather is beautiful today&quot;:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;It is sunny outside&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0.6</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Note: Actual scores may vary based on the specific METEOR implementation and parameters used.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="f-score">F-Score<a href="#f-score" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to F-Score" title="Direct link to F-Score" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>F-score (also F1 score) is used for measuring classification accuracy when you need to balance between being correct and being complete.</p>
<p><strong>Understanding Precision and Recall:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Precision</strong>: &quot;Of all the things I said were positive, how many actually were?&quot; (avoiding false alarms)</li>
<li class=""><strong>Recall</strong>: &quot;Of all the things that were positive, how many did I catch?&quot; (avoiding missed cases)</li>
<li class=""><strong>F-score</strong>: The harmonic mean that balances both - high only when BOTH are good</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>When to use F-score:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Classification tasks</strong>: Sentiment analysis, intent detection, category assignment</li>
<li class=""><strong>Imbalanced datasets</strong>: When some categories are rare and you can&#x27;t just optimize for accuracy</li>
<li class=""><strong>Quality + Coverage</strong>: When you need the model to be both accurate AND comprehensive</li>
</ul>
<p>See <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F1_score" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Wikipedia</a> for mathematical details.</p>
<p>F-score uses the <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/#defining-named-metrics">named metrics</a> and <a class="" href="/docs/configuration/expected-outputs/#creating-derived-metrics">derived metrics</a> features.</p>
<p>To calculate F-score, you first need to track the base classification metrics. We can do this using JavaScript assertions, for example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Track true positives, false positives, etc</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> javascript</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;output.sentiment === &#x27;positive&#x27; &amp;&amp; context.vars.sentiment === &#x27;positive&#x27; ? 1 : 0&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">metric</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> true_positives</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">weight</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> javascript</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;output.sentiment === &#x27;positive&#x27; &amp;&amp; context.vars.sentiment === &#x27;negative&#x27; ? 1 : 0&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">metric</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> false_positives</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">weight</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> javascript</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;output.sentiment === &#x27;negative&#x27; &amp;&amp; context.vars.sentiment === &#x27;positive&#x27; ? 1 : 0&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">metric</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> false_negatives</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">weight</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Then define derived metrics to calculate precision, recall and F-score:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">derivedMetrics</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Precision = TP / (TP + FP)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> precision</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> true_positives / (true_positives + false_positives)</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Recall = TP / (TP + FN)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> recall</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> true_positives / (true_positives + false_negatives)</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># F1 Score = 2 * (precision * recall) / (precision + recall)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">name</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> f1_score</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> 2 * true_positives / (2 * true_positives + false_positives + false_negatives)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The F-score will be calculated automatically after the eval completes. A score closer to 1 indicates better performance.</p>
<p>This is particularly useful for evaluating classification tasks like sentiment analysis, where you want to measure both the precision (accuracy of positive predictions) and recall (ability to find all positive cases).</p>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/promptfoo/promptfoo/tree/main/examples/f-score" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Github</a> for a complete example.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="finish-reason">Finish Reason<a href="#finish-reason" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Finish Reason" title="Direct link to Finish Reason" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>The <code>finish-reason</code> assertion checks if the model stopped generating for the expected reason. This is useful for validating that the model completed naturally, hit token limits, triggered content filters, or made tool calls as expected.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="standard-finish-reasons">Standard Finish Reasons<a href="#standard-finish-reasons" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Standard Finish Reasons" title="Direct link to Standard Finish Reasons" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>Models can stop generating for various reasons, which are normalized to these standard values:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong><code>stop</code></strong>: Natural completion (reached end of response, stop sequence matched)</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>length</code></strong>: Token limit reached (max_tokens exceeded, context length reached)</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>content_filter</code></strong>: Content filtering triggered due to safety policies</li>
<li class=""><strong><code>tool_calls</code></strong>: Model made function/tool calls</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-usage-1">Basic Usage<a href="#basic-usage-1" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Usage" title="Direct link to Basic Usage" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> finish</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">reason</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> stop </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Expects natural completion</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="common-examples">Common Examples<a href="#common-examples" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Common Examples" title="Direct link to Common Examples" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p><strong>Test for natural completion:</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tests</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">vars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Write a short poem about nature&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">assert</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> finish</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain">reason</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> stop </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Should complete naturally</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Test for token limit:</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule"
